PROGRAM!!! YOU CAN NEVER LOSE WHAT YOU DONATE, AND YOU ARE NOT TAKING A RISK!</strong></p>\n<p>This is a community of ordinary people, selflessly helping each other, a kind of mutual aid. This is the first sprout of something new in modern soulless and ruthless world of greed and hard cash. The goal here is not the money. The goal is to <strong>ACQUIRE AS MUCH AS YOU CAN</strong>. Financial Apocalypse! Before you join, be sure to be acquainted with our<strong> <a href=\"http://nnn-office.com/ideology/\" target=\"_blank\">IDEOLOGY</a>!</strong></p>\n<h3>The way it works:</h3>\n<p>You start by registering, enter your bank account details(where you will receive money) then you click on Donate to make a donation with your spare money. You will have to wait over a week to be matched with another participant who needs help, you will pay to this participant’s account and submit your proof of payment on the portal. The participant that received your donation will have to verify the payment on the portal before the transaction is marked as complete. Your navros keep growing for three weeks, then you can make a request to get help where &nbsp;participants will be matched to pay you your money plus additional 35% profit. For example, if you started with 100k, you will be getting 135k plus other bonuses if you qualify for any.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<h3 class=\"text-center\">NAVROS GROWTH ANALOGY</h3>\n<p><strong>Donated Navros frozen period</strong>: 14 days</p>\n<p><strong>Growths</strong>: 35%(Naira) &amp; 55% Bitcoin in 21 days</p>\n<p><strong>Referral Bonus:</strong> grows same way as Navros.</p>\n<p><strong>Other Bonuses</strong>: Do not grow.</p>\n<p><strong>Bonus Frozen Period</strong>: All bonus are frozen for 21 days.</p>\n<p><em>Frozen means you cannot withdraw it yet.</em></p>\n<p><strong>Remember the war against fake POP is is still on!&nbsp;</strong></p>\n<p>This is the last message we sent to a user that uploaded fake POP:</p>\n<p><em>Dear NNN participant, class=\"entry-header\">\n\t\t<h1 class=\"entry-title\">How to register in NNN</h1>\t</header><!-- .entry-header -->\n\n\t<div class=\"entry-content\">\n\t\t<div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-4\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>If you want to be a part of the Community, you should register on the official NNN&nbsp;website.</p>\n<p>To register in NNN you need to go to NNN-Nigeria&nbsp;website [<strong><a href=\"http://nnn-office.com\"><u>nnn-office.com</u></a></strong>] and click on “Registration” button.</p>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-8\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_center\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure 640px\"></div>\n\t\t</figure>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div><div class=\"vc_row wpb_row vc_row-fluid\"><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-12\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\"><div class=\"vc_separator wpb_content_element vc_separator_align_center vc_sep_width_100 vc_sep_border_width_2 vc_sep_pos_align_center vc_separator_no_text \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_text_column wpb_content_element \">\n\t\t<div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t\t\t<p>Fill the registration form as shown on screenshot:<br>\n(Fields marked with <span style=\"color: red;\">*</span> are required)</p>\n<ol>\n<li>Enter your name (or a nickname).</li>\n<li>Enter your e-mail (preferable mailbox is gmail.com).</li>\n<li>Enter your mobile phone number</li>\n<li>Enter your Referrer’s email (optional)</li>\n<li>Enter how you heard about us. (Optional)</li>\n<li><b>Necessarily</b> read the <a style=\"color: red;\" href=\"http://nnn-office.com/warning\">WARNING</a> and check the box that you accept it.</li>\n<li>Create your password</li>\n<li>Retype created password</li>\n<li>Click on “Join Now” button.</li>\n</ol>\n\n\t\t</div>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div><div class=\"wpb_column vc_column_container vc_col-sm-7\"><div class=\"vc_column-inner \"><div class=\"wpb_wrapper\">\n\t<div class=\"wpb_single_image wpb_content_element vc_align_center\">\n\t\t\n\t\t<figure class=\"wpb_wrapper vc_figure\">\n\t\t\t<div class=\"vc_single_image-wrapper   vc_box_border_grey\"><img width=\"591\" height=\"634\" src=\"https://nnn-office.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/register2.png\" class=\"vc_single_image-img attachment-large\" alt=\"\" srcset=\"https://nnn-office.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/register2.png 591w, https://nnn-office.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/10/register2-280x300.png 280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 591px) 100vw, 591px\"></div>\n\t\t</figure>\n\t</div>\n</div></div></div></div>\n<div style=\"margin:0\"><b>Tell your Friends and Get 10 percent of their donations</b></div><style>.fballshare_left {float:left;}.fballshare { margin: 0px; It was an improved MMM system- there will be no moratorium and the system will be automated. No body can control your account or hack your account.\n\nNNN Ai was developed in India in June 2016. In Feb 2016, a team of developers working with NNN founders decided an online platform and NNN Nigeria Website was launched in August 2016.
